<p class="gb-text gbp-section__text gb-text-701f3a7d">Skip the overwhelm. Get custom itineraries, curated guides, and insider advice on the trails, tastes, and traditions most visitors miss.</p>

<h2 class="gb-headline gb-headline-c6ad2351 gb-headline-text">Your Path to Adventure + Culture</h2>



<p class="gb-headline gb-headline-66b59212 gb-headline-text"><strong>Hi, we&#8217;re Kate &amp; Vin</strong> — For over 11 years, we’ve been hiking, mapping, and mastering <a href="https://throneandvine.com/why-visit-south-tyrol/"><strong>South Tyrol</strong></a> and the <a href="https://throneandvine.com/dolomites/"><strong>Dolomites</strong></a> — discovering which trails are worth the climb, which valleys stay quiet, and which local experiences turn a good trip into an unforgettable one.</p>



<p>Most travel advice online is generic. Ours comes from a decade of boots-on-the-ground experience. <strong>We’ve helped thousands of travelers skip the guesswork and move through the region like insiders.</strong> Whether you need a <a href="https://throneandvine.com/south-tyrol-dolomites-custom-itinerary-service/"><strong>custom itinerary</strong></a>, a trail-tested <a href="https://throneandvine.com/south-tyrol-travel-guides/"><strong>hiking guide</strong></a>, or just clear, honest <a href="https://throneandvine.com/south-tyrol-trip-consultation-call/"><strong>advice on where to stay</strong></a>, we turn logistical headaches into seamless adventures.</p>
